        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üéâ We‚Äôre proud to share that <a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/in/softwareprocurement?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Aamer Trambu</a>, Senior Consultant in our ITAM Managed Services team at <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>, has been shortlisted as a finalist for Consultant of the Year at the <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/itam-forum?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>ITAM FORUM</a> Excellence Awards!

¬†
Please join us in congratulating Aamer on this fantastic achievement, and wishing him the very best of luck ahead of the awards in November. üëè

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üìä Speaker Spotlight: <a class="link" href="https://ie.linkedin.com/in/egbertij?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Egbert IJsseldijk</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/google-cloud/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Google Cloud</a> GTM Lead at <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>.
¬†
‚ÄúThe biggest opportunity organizations miss is compounding intelligence.‚Äù
¬†
As Egbert explains, when sales, marketing, finance, and customer data all sit in <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsilos&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#silos</a>, innovation and efficiency stall. Connecting those data points unlocks true business outcomes and customer value.
¬†
At the <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> Summit 2025 on October 23, Egbert will host ‚ÄúThe Engine that Turns Data into Your Advantage,‚Äù exploring how an AI-native approach with analytics, ML, and agents helps organizations automate workflows, surface insights, and innovate securely at scale.
¬†

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üèÜ WE WON!!! üèÜ

What a dazzling night at the 10th Employer Brand Management Awards 2025 by <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/communicate-magazine?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Communicate magazine</a> in London.

On 24 September, <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> proudly won:

üèÖGold: Best Employer Brand Management (Technology, Media &amp; Telecommunications).

The judges called our work ‚Äúa compelling, authentic approach that balances global consistency with local relevance.‚Äù

ü•àSilver Best Localisation Programme, alongside <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/amdocs?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Amdocs</a> (Gold) and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/boston-consulting-group?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Boston Consulting Group (BCG)</a> (Bronze). Judges praised it as ‚Äúhighly impactful and culturally attuned.‚Äù

These awards are among the most respected in the employer-branding world, judged via a rigorous evaluation process led by industry leaders.

This win celebrates the heartbeat of our brand, our stories, our videos, the vibrant <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fswocareers&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SWOCareers</a> community, and the TA campaigns that turn creativity into real career opportunities.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">üöß You can‚Äôt build <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> on shaky cloud foundations.¬†
¬†
AI can‚Äôt succeed without secure, scalable, and well-governed infrastructure in place first, and that‚Äôs where cloud landing zones come in. 

In our latest blog, we share four real-world stories that show how <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a> helped organizations build the foundations they needed for successful cloud initiatives cross <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/microsoft-azure/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Microsoft Azure</a>, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/amazon-web-services?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Amazon Web Services (AWS)</a>, and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/google-cloud/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Google Cloud</a>.

üí° <a class="link" href="https://au.linkedin.com/company/grill'd-pty-ltd?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Grill'd</a> Healthy Burgers (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fazure&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Azure</a>)¬†- Cut costs by 30% while enabling secure growth and innovation. 

üí° <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/artfund?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Art Fund</a> (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fawscloud&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AWSCloud</a>)¬†- Implemented a compliant, secure AWS landing zone as a platform to improve stakeholder experience and resilience.

üí° Altadia Group (<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fgooglecloud&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#GoogleCloud</a>)¬†
Seamlessly migrated <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsap&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SAP</a> to Google Cloud with near-zero disruption, unlocking analytics potential. 

üí°<a class="link" href="https://ua.linkedin.com/company/dtek?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>DTEK</a>K (AWS Cloud)¬†
Delivered a robust AWS landing zone to support critical infrastructure operations, setting the stage for secure, AI-enabled innovation. 

Each one story is proof that success in the cloud requires solid foundations, and AI is no exception!

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Giving back is in our DNA.

At <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/softwareone?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SoftwareOne</a>, we‚Äôve always believed that doing good is part of doing business. And as we continue our journey forward with <a class="link" href="https://no.linkedin.com/company/crayon-group?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Crayon</a> as one company, it‚Äôs clear that this commitment to people and communities is something we share deeply.

Through initiatives like <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsoftwareonegivesback&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SoftwareOneGivesBack</a> and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fcrayoncares&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#CrayonCares</a>, our teams around the world have supported causes that align with our values, from feeding schoolchildren in Africa and Europe, to providing trauma counselling in Ukraine, and protecting rainforests across the globe.

As one organization, we‚Äôre combining our strengths and expanding our reach, supporting global and local projects that reflect our shared ESG priorities: sustainability, inclusion, health, education, and using technology for good.

üåç It‚Äôs not just about giving. It‚Äôs about impact.
